# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
circle is all points with distance r from center c ^OCpLc6Uw

the unit or average cost is the cost of producing a certain ammount of units, the marginal cost
is the change in the cost per unit with the change of unit produced. ^eUCQaZdV

if function is concave up, derivative goes from negative to positive and always grow so second derivative always positive ^YYAYjSC8

opposite for concave down ^QoNL7STg

if scond derivative touches 0 local point concavity changes with local point of inflection ^xbZwneTz
